If statement included

{which (is.na(a) & is.na(b))}

pos_na
function (a, b) 
{
    if (length(a) == length(b)) {
        which(is.na(a) & is.na(b))
    }
    else {
        print("The vectors are not the same length.")
    }
}
x <- c(1, NA, 2) 
y <- c(NA, NA)
pos_na(x,y)

Without if statement

#Let's start by establishing a pos_na2 variable for the if not statement. 


pos_na2 <- function(x, y, na.rm = FALSE) {
  stopifnot(length(x) == length(y))
  return(which(is.na(x) & is.na(y)))
}

pos_na2
function (x, y, na.rm = FALSE) 
{
    stopifnot(length(x) == length(y))
    return(which(is.na(x) & is.na(y)))
}

Proportion calculation

wmata_data2|>
  group_by(Month,Wday)|>
  mutate(Proportion = Total/sum(Total))|>
  ungroup()-> wmata_data2

head(wmata_data2)
# A tibble: 6 × 6
  Date        Total  Year Month Wday  Proportion
  <chr>       <int> <dbl> <dbl> <ord>      <dbl>
1 2006-01-01 121000  2006     1 Sun      0.0120 
2 2006-01-02 157000  2006     1 Mon      0.00524
3 2006-01-03 583000  2006     1 Tue      0.0156 
4 2006-01-04 626000  2006     1 Wed      0.0166 
5 2006-01-05 638000  2006     1 Thu      0.0170 
6 2006-01-06 636000  2006     1 Fri      0.0177

Boxplot for proportions

ggplot(wmata_data2, aes(x = Wday, y = Proportion)) +
  geom_boxplot()

Question 3

Subset by index

V <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")


names(V) <- c("b", "l", "d", "e", "be")

V[c("b", "d", "be")]
         b          d         be 
   "Bears" "Dolphins"  "Bengals"

Subsetting for loop

#Subsetting for loop

V <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")

for (i in c(1,3,5)) {
  print (V[i])
}
[1] "Bears"
[1] "Dolphins"
[1] "Bengals"

Subsetting with positive indices

V <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")


V[c(1, 3, 5)]
[1] "Bears"    "Dolphins" "Bengals"

Subsetting using negative indices

V <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")

V[-c(2,4)]
[1] "Bears"    "Dolphins" "Bengals"

Subsetting using logical indexing

V <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")

V[c(TRUE, FALSE, TRUE, FALSE, TRUE)]
[1] "Bears"    "Dolphins" "Bengals"

Subsetting by names

names(V) <- c("Bears", "Lions", "Dolphins", "Eagles", "Bengals")

V[c("Bears", "Dolphins", "Bengals")]
     Bears   Dolphins    Bengals 
   "Bears" "Dolphins"  "Bengals"

Question 4

Parse

records <- c(
  "Steve McQueen | 2020-01-15 | HR",
  "B. Smith | 15/02/2021 | FIN",
  "Carlos M | March 3, 2019 | IT",
  "D. Lee | 2018/07/30 | HR",
  "Alain Delon | 04-12-2020 | MKT"
)
records
[1] "Steve McQueen | 2020-01-15 | HR" "B. Smith | 15/02/2021 | FIN"    
[3] "Carlos M | March 3, 2019 | IT"   "D. Lee | 2018/07/30 | HR"       
[5] "Alain Delon | 04-12-2020 | MKT"

Parse into three separate variables

HRData <- tibble(records = c( "Steve McQueen | 2020-01-15 | HR",
  "B. Smith | 15/02/2021 | FIN",
  "Carlos M | March 3, 2019 | IT",
  "D. Lee | 2018/07/30 | HR",
  "Alain Delon | 04-12-2020 | MKT"))
                 
HRData |>              
separate_wider_delim(records,
                     names = c("name", "hire_date", "dept"),
                     delim = "|")
# A tibble: 5 × 3
  name             hire_date         dept  
  <chr>            <chr>             <chr> 
1 "Steve McQueen " " 2020-01-15 "    " HR" 
2 "B. Smith "      " 15/02/2021 "    " FIN"
3 "Carlos M "      " March 3, 2019 " " IT" 
4 "D. Lee "        " 2018/07/30 "    " HR" 
5 "Alain Delon "   " 04-12-2020 "    " MKT"

Convert dates

ymd("2020-01-15")

[1] "2021-02-15"

[1] "2019-03-03"
ymd("2018/07/30")
[1] "2018-07-30"
mdy("4-12-2020")
[1] "2020-04-12"
hire_date <- c("2020-01-15", "2021-02-15", "2019-03-03","2018-07-30", "2020-04-12")

hire_date
[1] "2020-01-15" "2021-02-15" "2019-03-03" "2018-07-30" "2020-04-12"

x1 <- c("HR", "FIN", "IT", "HR", "MKT")

x1
[1] "HR"  "FIN" "IT"  "HR"  "MKT"

Construct a data frame

hire_date <- c ("2020-01-15","2021-02-15","2019-03-03","2018-07-30","2020-04-12")

dept <- c("FIN","HR","IT","MKT")

name <- c("Steve McQueen", "B.Smith", "Carlos M", "D. Lee", "Alain Delon")


clean_df <- data.frame(
  hire_date = c("2020-01-15","2021-02-15","2019-03-03","2018-07-30","2020-04-12"), 
  dept = c("HR","FIN","IT","HR","MKT"), 
  name = c("Steve McQueen", "B.Smith", "Carlos M", "D. Lee", "Alain Delon")
)

clean_df

2 2021-02-15  FIN       B.Smith
3 2019-03-03   IT      Carlos M
4 2018-07-30   HR        D. Lee
5 2020-04-12  MKT   Alain Delon

Add a new variable: years worked

Include new variable into refined data frame

clean_df <- data.frame(
  hire_date = c("2020-01-15","2021-02-15","2019-03-03","2018-07-30","2020-04-12"), 
  dept = c("HR","FIN","IT","HR","MKT"), 
  name = c("Steve McQueen", "B.Smith", "Carlos M", "D. Lee", "Alain Delon"),
  years_worked = c("6.09", "5", "6.96", "7.55", "5.85")
) -> clean_df2

clean_df2
   hire_date dept          name years_worked
1 2020-01-15   HR Steve McQueen         6.09
2 2021-02-15  FIN       B.Smith            5
3 2019-03-03   IT      Carlos M         6.96
4 2018-07-30   HR        D. Lee         7.55
5 2020-04-12  MKT   Alain Delon         5.85
